       26 +## How it works (practical walkthrough)                       
       27 +                                                              
       28 +```                                                           
       29 +1. ap run <target>        # profile with samply, symbolicate, 
          +rank hot functions                                            
       30 +        │                 #   → token-budgeted "context bundle
          +": top hotspots, crate                                        
       31 +        │                 #     rollup, source snippets, why-h
          +ot tags  (md or json)                                         
       32 +        ▼                                                     
       33 +2. LLM reads the bundle   # picks ONE hot function it owns, pr
          +oposes an optimization                                        
       34 +        ▼                                                     
       35 +3. cargo test  (or a deterministic output fingerprint for exte
          +rnal targets)                                                 
       36 +        │  fail → git checkout (revert), log "rejected", next 
       37 +        ▼ pass                                                
       38 +4. ap bench <target>      # quiesced min-of-N wall-clock + pea
          +k RAM, per dataset                                            
       39 +        │  not >3% faster, or a guard dataset regressed, or ov
          +er RAM budget → revert                                        
       40 +        ▼ win

      107 +## The optimize loop (sequence view)                          
      108 +                                                              
      109 +```mermaid                                                    
      110 +sequenceDiagram                                               
      111 +  autonumber                                                  
      112 +  participant W as Improve loop                               
      113 +  participant AP as ap (profiler/bench)                       
      114 +  participant T as Target repo                                
      115 +  participant G as Gates                                      
      116 +  participant D as Dashboard data                             
      117 +                                                              
      118 +  W->>AP: ap run (profile + symbolicate)                      
      119 +  AP-->>W: context bundle (ranked hotspots + source)          
      120 +  W->>T: edit ONE hot function                                
      121 +  W->>G: cargo test  /  output fingerprint                    
      122 +  alt correctness fails                                       
      123 +    G-->>W: FAIL                                              
      124 +    W->>T: git checkout (revert)                              
      125 +    W->>D: activity "rejected: <reason>"                      
      126 +  else correctness holds                                      
      127 +    W->>AP: ap bench (quiesced min-of-N + peak RAM)           
      128 +    AP-->>G: Δtime, ΔRAM vs baseline                          
      129 +    alt >3% faster, no guard regression, under RAM budget     
      130 +      W->>T: git commit (local only)                          
      131 +      W->>D: bench point + findings + activity "accepted"     
      132 +    else not enough / regressed                               
      133 +      W->>T: git checkout (revert)                            
      134 +      W->>D: activity "rejected: <reason>"                    
      135 +    end                                                       
      136 +  end                                                         
      137 +```                                                           
      138 +                                                              
      139 +## Swarm tournament (when one approach isn't enough)          
      140 +                                                              
      141 +```mermaid                                                    
      142 +flowchart TD                                                  
      143 +  H["hot path"] --> G1["lens: locality"] & G2["lens: dedup cop
          +ies"] & G3["lens: algorithmic"]                               
      144 +  G1 & G2 & G3 -->|"parallel · read-only · propose patch"| P[(
          +"/tmp candidates")]                                           
      145 +  P --> E["serial, quiesced:<br/>apply → test → bench → revert
          +"]                                                            
      146 +  E --> J{"best clears<br/>gate?"}                            
      147 +  J -->|yes| C["commit winner"]                               
      148 +  J -->|no| K["keep baseline<br/>(honest no-op)"]             
      149 +```                                                           
      150 +                                                              
      151 +Ideas are generated **in parallel** (cheap, read-only); evalua
          +tion is **serial and                                          
      152 +quiesced** so the benchmark that decides the winner is never s
          +kewed by contention.                                          
      153 +                                                              
      154 +---                                                           
      155 +                                                              
      156 +## Why the gates are trustworthy                              
      157 +                                                              
      158 +- **Correctness is ground truth, not vibes.** Internal target 
          +→ the real `cargo test`                                       
      159 +  suite. External target (polars) → a deterministic **fingerpr
          +int** of the workload's                                       
      160 +  output (value sum + exact row count + order-sensitive checks
          +um) that must match the                                       
      161 +  baseline bit-for-bit. The baseline output is assumed correct
          + unless a bug is *proven*.                                    
      162 +- **Timing is honest.** Benchmarks are min-of-N, taken seriall
          +y with nothing else running;                                  
      163 +  improvements must clear a threshold beyond noise, and guard 
          +datasets must not regress.                                    
      164 +- **Memory is budgeted.** Peak RSS (and optional dhat heap) is
          + recorded per commit; a                                       
      165 +  change may trade memory for speed only under an explicit RAM
          + ceiling.                                                     
      166 +                                                              
      167 +See [`autonomous-profiler/README.md`](autonomous-profiler/READ
          +ME.md) for the full CLI/MCP                                   
      168 +reference and internals.

  1. Side-effect analysis — clean (proof in the highlight): resolve_chunked_idx
  is a private, pure function with exactly two callers, both in gather.rs. The
  two code paths are mathematically identical for every input — for a monotone
  predicate over the sorted cumlens, the new linear "count of trues" equals
  partition_point exactly (including empty-chunk/duplicate cases), so it returns
  bit-for-bit identical (chunk, offset). A pure function with identical output
  can't produce side effects. The fingerprint over 2.96M rows already matched
  the baseline exactly.

  2. Highlight page (highlights/polars-resolve-chunked-idx.md): the diff, why
  it's faster (per-element call, tiny chunk arrays → branchless linear scan
  beats binary search; >8 fallback preserves O(log n)), and the full correctness
  proof + no-side-effects argument.

⏺ Meta-loop launched (whl1mf20y) — building on the 7 wins (flights at 235 ms).

  How it'll run, up to 3 rounds, each:
  1. 5 lenses propose in parallel (algorithmic · locality · dedup · data-shape ·
  branch-flatten) — read-only, picking different functions (the 7
  already-optimized are off-limits).
  2. Serial gated eval — apply → cargo test → quiesced bench (flights +
  transactions) → revert.
  3. Commit the round's winner (>3% flights, no >2% txn regression, tests
  green), update the baseline, then go again.
  4. Stop when a round goes dry (nothing beats the new baseline) or after
  round 3.

  Watch the Activity tab — run labels swarm-r1, swarm-r2, swarm-r3; you'll see
  each lens report tests / flights% / txn%, the round winner land a green bar,
  then the next round kick off against the raised bar.

  high and later rounds will likely go dry — which is the meta-loop working, not
